         <section class="zsg-content-section " id="hdp-neighborhood">
          <h2>
           Neighborhood: Grant
          </h2>
          <div class="zsg-content-component">
           <div class="za-track-event zsg-content-component notranslate" data-za-action="Market Guide - expand" data-za-category="Homes">
            Zillow predicts 80302 home values will increase 1.7% next year, compared to a 0.9% rise for Boulder as a whole. Among 80302 homes, this home is 590.6% more expensive than the midpoint (median) home, and is priced 133.5% more per
            <span class="hide" id="util_TextFold_0_toggleArea">
             square foot.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             Foreclosures will be a factor impacting home values in the next several years.  In 80302, the number of foreclosures waiting to be sold is 83.3% lower than in Boulder, and 96.2% lower than the national average. This lower local number could help 80302 home values rise more quickly than other regions in Boulder.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             Learn more about
             <a href="https://zillow.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/203517190-How-are-Zillow-Home-Value-Forecasts-calculated-">
              forecast calculations
             </a>
             or
             <a href="http://www.zillow.com/co-80302/home-values/">
              80302 home values
             </a>
